Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On </span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#212529;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">July 21, 2023</span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">, GameStop Corp. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) was informed by </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Diana Saadeh-Jajeh</span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">, the Company&#8217;s Chief Financial Officer, that she will resign from such position effective August 11, 2023</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">. Ms. Saadeh-Jajeh&#8217;s resignation was not because of any disagreement with the Company on any matter relating to the Company&#8217;s operations, policies or practices, including accounting principles and practices.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On July 27, 2023, in connection with Ms. Saadeh-Jajeh&#8217;s resignation, the Board appointed Daniel Moore as the Company&#8217;s Principal Accounting Officer and interim Principal Financial Officer effective August 11, 2023.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Moore, 40 years old, has served as the Company&#8217;s Vice President, Corporate Global Controller since September 2022, and as Vice President, Global Tax since July 2021.  Prior to joining the Company in 2021, Mr. Moore held the position of Vice President, Tax at Elevate Textiles, and Director of International Tax at Roper Technologies.  Overall, Mr. Moore has over 18 years&#8217; experience in accounting and tax.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">No family relationships exist between Mr. Moore and any of the Company&#8217;s directors or other executive officers. There are no other arrangements between Mr. Moore and any other person pursuant to which he was selected as an officer, nor are there any transactions to which the Company is or was a participant and in which Mr. Moore has a material interest subject to disclosure under Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div
